\DoxyCodeLine{00274\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00275\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ This\ part\ deals\ with\ the\ special\ case\ where\ a\ unit\ wants\ to\ inline\ xxHash,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00276\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ but\ "{}xxhash.h"{}\ has\ previously\ been\ included\ without\ XXH\_INLINE\_ALL,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00277\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ such\ as\ part\ of\ some\ previously\ included\ *.h\ header\ file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00278\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ Without\ further\ action,\ the\ new\ include\ would\ just\ be\ ignored,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00279\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ and\ functions\ would\ effectively\ \_not\_\ be\ inlined\ (silent\ failure).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00280\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ The\ following\ macros\ solve\ this\ situation\ by\ prefixing\ all\ inlined\ names,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00281\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ avoiding\ naming\ collision\ with\ previous\ inclusions.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00282\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00283\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Before\ that,\ we\ unconditionally\ \#undef\ all\ symbols,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00284\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ in\ case\ they\ were\ already\ defined\ with\ XXH\_NAMESPACE.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00285\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ *\ They\ will\ then\ be\ redefined\ for\ XXH\_INLINE\_ALL}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00286\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00688\ \textcolor{comment}{/*******\ \ \ Canonical\ representation\ \ \ *******/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00689\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00690\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00691\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ default\ return\ values\ from\ XXH\ functions\ are\ unsigned\ 32\ and\ 64\ bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00692\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ integers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00693\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ the\ simplest\ and\ fastest\ format\ for\ further\ post-\/processing.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00694\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00695\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ this\ leaves\ open\ the\ question\ of\ what\ is\ the\ order\ on\ the\ byte\ level,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00696\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ since\ little\ and\ big\ endian\ conventions\ will\ store\ the\ same\ number\ differently.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00697\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00698\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ canonical\ representation\ settles\ this\ issue\ by\ mandating\ big-\/endian}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00699\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ convention,\ the\ same\ convention\ as\ human-\/readable\ numbers\ (large\ digits\ first).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00700\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00701\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ When\ writing\ hash\ values\ to\ storage,\ sending\ them\ over\ a\ network,\ or\ printing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00702\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ them,\ it's\ highly\ recommended\ to\ use\ the\ canonical\ representation\ to\ ensure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00703\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ portability\ across\ a\ wider\ range\ of\ systems,\ present\ and\ future.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00704\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00705\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ following\ functions\ allow\ transformation\ of\ hash\ values\ to\ and\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00706\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ canonical\ format.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00707\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00708\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00712\ \textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{00713\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}\ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{struct_x_x_h32__canonical__t_a85a83578344a5dd1c7a6cc0472230f30}{digest}}[4];\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{00714\ \}\ \doxymbox{\hyperlink{struct_x_x_h32__canonical__t}{XXH32\_canonical\_t}};}

\DoxyCodeLine{01750\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01751\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{01752\ \textcolor{comment}{/*-\/**********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash\ implementation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *-\/**********************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash's\ implementation\ used\ to\ be\ hosted\ inside\ xxhash.c.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ inlining\ requires\ implementation\ to\ be\ visible\ to\ the\ compiler,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ hence\ be\ included\ alongside\ the\ header.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Previously,\ implementation\ was\ hosted\ inside\ xxhash.c,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ which\ was\ then\ \#included\ when\ inlining\ was\ activated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01761\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ construction\ created\ issues\ with\ a\ few\ build\ and\ install\ systems,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01762\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ as\ it\ required\ xxhash.c\ to\ be\ stored\ in\ /include\ directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01763\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01764\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxHash\ implementation\ is\ now\ directly\ integrated\ within\ xxhash.h.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01765\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ As\ a\ consequence,\ xxhash.c\ is\ no\ longer\ needed\ in\ /include.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01766\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01767\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxhash.c\ is\ still\ available\ and\ is\ still\ useful.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01768\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ a\ "{}normal"{}\ setup,\ when\ xxhash\ is\ not\ inlined,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01769\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ xxhash.h\ only\ exposes\ the\ prototypes\ and\ public\ symbols,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02585\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ xxh\_u32\ XXH32\_round(xxh\_u32\ acc,\ xxh\_u32\ input)}
\DoxyCodeLine{02586\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{02587\ \ \ \ \ acc\ +=\ input\ *\ XXH\_PRIME32\_2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02588\ \ \ \ \ acc\ \ =\ XXH\_rotl32(acc,\ 13);}
\DoxyCodeLine{02589\ \ \ \ \ acc\ *=\ XXH\_PRIME32\_1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{02590\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ (defined(\_\_SSE4\_1\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_aarch64\_\_)\ ||\ defined(\_\_wasm\_simd128\_\_))\ \&\&\ !defined(XXH\_ENABLE\_AUTOVECTORIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02591\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02592\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ UGLY\ HACK:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02593\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ A\ compiler\ fence\ is\ the\ only\ thing\ that\ prevents\ GCC\ and\ Clang\ from}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02594\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ autovectorizing\ the\ XXH32\ loop\ (pragmas\ and\ attributes\ don't\ work\ for\ some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02595\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ reason)\ without\ globally\ disabling\ SSE4.1.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02596\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02597\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ The\ reason\ we\ want\ to\ avoid\ vectorization\ is\ because\ despite\ working\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02598\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ 4\ integers\ at\ a\ time,\ there\ are\ multiple\ factors\ slowing\ XXH32\ down\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02599\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ SSE4:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02600\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ -\/\ There's\ a\ ridiculous\ amount\ of\ lag\ from\ pmulld\ (10\ cycles\ of\ latency\ on}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02601\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ newer\ chips!)\ making\ it\ slightly\ slower\ to\ multiply\ four\ integers\ at}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02602\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ once\ compared\ to\ four\ integers\ independently.\ Even\ when\ pmulld\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02603\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ fastest,\ Sandy/Ivy\ Bridge,\ it\ is\ still\ not\ worth\ it\ to\ go\ into\ SSE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02604\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ just\ to\ multiply\ unless\ doing\ a\ long\ operation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02605\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02606\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ -\/\ Four\ instructions\ are\ required\ to\ rotate,}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02619\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03446\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{03447\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03448\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ One\ goal\ of\ XXH3\ is\ to\ make\ it\ fast\ on\ both\ 32-\/bit\ and\ 64-\/bit,\ while}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03449\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ remaining\ a\ true\ 64-\/bit/128-\/bit\ hash\ function.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03450\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03451\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ done\ by\ prioritizing\ a\ subset\ of\ 64-\/bit\ operations\ that\ can\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03452\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emulated\ without\ too\ many\ steps\ on\ the\ average\ 32-\/bit\ machine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03453\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03454\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ these\ two\ lines\ seem\ similar,\ and\ run\ equally\ fast\ on\ 64-\/bit:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03455\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03456\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ xxh\_u64\ x;}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03457\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 47);\ //\ good}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03458\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 13);\ //\ bad}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03459\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03460\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ to\ a\ 32-\/bit\ machine,\ there\ is\ a\ major\ difference.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03461\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03462\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 47)\ looks\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03463\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03464\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.lo\ \string^=\ (x.hi\ >>\ (47\ -\/\ 32));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03465\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03466\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ while\ x\ \string^=\ (x\ >>\ 13)\ looks\ like\ this:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03467\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03468\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ //\ note:\ funnel\ shifts\ are\ not\ usually\ cheap.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03469\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.lo\ \string^=\ (x.lo\ >>\ 13)\ |\ (x.hi\ <<\ (32\ -\/\ 13));}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03470\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ x.hi\ \string^=\ (x.hi\ >>\ 13);}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03471\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03472\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ first\ one\ is\ significantly\ faster\ than\ the\ second,\ simply\ because\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03473\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ shift\ is\ larger\ than\ 32.\ This\ means:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03474\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ All\ the\ bits\ we\ need\ are\ in\ the\ upper\ 32\ bits,\ so\ we\ can\ ignore\ the\ lower}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03475\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ 32\ bits\ in\ the\ shift.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03476\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ The\ shift\ result\ will\ always\ fit\ in\ the\ lower\ 32\ bits,\ and\ therefore,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03477\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ we\ can\ ignore\ the\ upper\ 32\ bits\ in\ the\ xor.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03478\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03479\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thanks\ to\ this\ optimization,\ XXH3\ only\ requires\ these\ features\ to\ be\ efficient:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03480\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03481\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ Usable\ unaligned\ access}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03482\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ A\ 32-\/bit\ or\ 64-\/bit\ ALU}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03483\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ -\/\ If\ 32-\/bit,\ a\ decent\ ADC\ instruction}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03484\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ A\ 32\ or\ 64-\/bit\ multiply\ with\ a\ 64-\/bit\ result}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03485\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ -\/\ For\ the\ 128-\/bit\ variant,\ a\ decent\ byteswap\ helps\ short\ inputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03486\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03487\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ first\ two\ are\ already\ required\ by\ XXH32,\ and\ almost\ all\ 32-\/bit\ and\ 64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03488\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ platforms\ which\ can\ run\ XXH32\ can\ run\ XXH3\ efficiently.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03489\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03490\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thumb-\/1,\ the\ classic\ 16-\/bit\ only\ subset\ of\ ARM's\ instruction\ set,\ is\ one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03491\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ notable\ exception.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03492\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03493\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ First\ of\ all,\ Thumb-\/1\ lacks\ support\ for\ the\ UMULL\ instruction\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03494\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ performs\ the\ important\ long\ multiply.\ This\ means\ numerous\ \_\_aeabi\_lmul}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03495\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03496\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03497\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Second\ of\ all,\ the\ 8\ functional\ registers\ are\ just\ not\ enough.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03498\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Setup\ for\ \_\_aeabi\_lmul,\ byteshift\ loads,\ pointers,\ and\ all\ arithmetic\ need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03499\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Lo\ registers,\ and\ this\ shuffling\ results\ in\ thousands\ more\ MOVs\ than\ A32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03500\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03501\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ A32\ and\ T32\ don't\ have\ this\ limitation.\ They\ can\ access\ all\ 14\ registers,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03502\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ do\ a\ 32-\/>64\ multiply\ with\ UMULL,\ and\ the\ flexible\ operand\ allowing\ free}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03503\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ shifts\ is\ helpful,\ too.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03504\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03505\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Therefore,\ we\ do\ a\ quick\ sanity\ check.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03506\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03507\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ If\ compiling\ Thumb-\/1\ for\ a\ target\ which\ supports\ ARM\ instructions,\ we\ will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03508\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emit\ a\ warning,\ as\ it\ is\ not\ a\ "{}sane"{}\ platform\ to\ compile\ for.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03509\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03510\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Usually,\ if\ this\ happens,\ it\ is\ because\ of\ an\ accident\ and\ you\ probably\ need}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03511\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ specify\ -\/march,\ as\ you\ likely\ meant\ to\ compile\ for\ a\ newer\ architecture.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03512\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03513\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Credit:\ large\ sections\ of\ the\ vectorial\ and\ asm\ source\ code\ paths}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03514\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ have\ been\ contributed\ by\ @easyaspi314}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03515\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03516\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ defined(\_\_thumb\_\_)\ \&\&\ !defined(\_\_thumb2\_\_)\ \&\&\ defined(\_\_ARM\_ARCH\_ISA\_ARM)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03517\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#\ \ \ warning\ "{}XXH3\ is\ highly\ inefficient\ without\ ARM\ or\ Thumb-\/2."{}}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03518\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03519\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{03521\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Vectorization\ detection}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03522\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{03663\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03664\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ UGLY\ HACK:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03665\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ GCC\ usually\ generates\ the\ best\ code\ with\ -\/O3\ for\ xxHash.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03666\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03667\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ when\ targeting\ AVX2,\ it\ is\ overzealous\ in\ its\ unrolling\ resulting}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03668\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ code\ roughly\ 3/4\ the\ speed\ of\ Clang.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03669\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03670\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ are\ other\ issues,\ such\ as\ GCC\ splitting\ \_mm256\_loadu\_si256\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03671\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \_mm\_loadu\_si128\ +\ \_mm256\_inserti128\_si256.\ This\ is\ an\ optimization\ which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03672\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ only\ applies\ to\ Sandy\ and\ Ivy\ Bridge...\ which\ don't\ even\ support\ AVX2.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03673\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03674\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ That\ is\ why\ when\ compiling\ the\ AVX2\ version,\ it\ is\ recommended\ to\ use\ either}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03675\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ -\/O2\ -\/mavx2\ -\/march=haswell}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03676\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03677\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ \ -\/O2\ -\/mavx2\ -\/mno-\/avx256-\/split-\/unaligned-\/load}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03678\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ for\ decent\ performance,\ or\ to\ use\ Clang\ instead.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03679\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03680\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Fortunately,\ we\ can\ control\ the\ first\ one\ with\ a\ pragma\ that\ forces\ GCC\ into}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03681\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ -\/O2,\ but\ the\ other\ one\ we\ can't\ control\ without\ "{}failed\ to\ inline\ always}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03682\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ inline\ function\ due\ to\ target\ mismatch"{}\ warnings.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03683\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{03684\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if\ XXH\_VECTOR\ ==\ XXH\_AVX2\ }\textcolor{comment}{/*\ AVX2\ */}\textcolor{preprocessor}{\ \(\backslash\)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04144\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ *\ \ \ \ \ of\ 32-\/bit\ ADD/ADCs.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04146\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{04216\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04217\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04218\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Short\ keys}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04219\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04220\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ One\ of\ the\ shortcomings\ of\ XXH32\ and\ XXH64\ was\ that\ their\ performance\ was}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04221\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ sub-\/optimal\ on\ short\ lengths.\ It\ used\ an\ iterative\ algorithm\ which\ strongly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04222\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ favored\ lengths\ that\ were\ a\ multiple\ of\ 4\ or\ 8.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04223\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04224\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Instead\ of\ iterating\ over\ individual\ inputs,\ we\ use\ a\ set\ of\ single\ shot}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04225\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions\ which\ piece\ together\ a\ range\ of\ lengths\ and\ operate\ in\ constant\ time.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04226\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04227\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Additionally,\ the\ number\ of\ multiplies\ has\ been\ significantly\ reduced.\ This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04228\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ reduces\ latency,\ especially\ when\ emulating\ 64-\/bit\ multiplies\ on\ 32-\/bit.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04229\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04230\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Depending\ on\ the\ platform,\ this\ may\ or\ may\ not\ be\ faster\ than\ XXH32,\ but\ it}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04231\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ is\ almost\ guaranteed\ to\ be\ faster\ than\ XXH64.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04232\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04233\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04234\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04235\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ At\ very\ short\ lengths,\ there\ isn't\ enough\ input\ to\ fully\ hide\ secrets,\ or\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04236\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ entire\ secret.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04237\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04238\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ There\ is\ also\ only\ a\ limited\ amount\ of\ mixing\ we\ can\ do\ before\ significantly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04239\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ impacting\ performance.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04240\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04241\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Therefore,\ we\ use\ different\ sections\ of\ the\ secret\ and\ always\ mix\ two\ secret}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04242\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ samples\ with\ an\ XOR.\ This\ should\ have\ no\ effect\ on\ performance\ on\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04243\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ seedless\ or\ withSeed\ variants\ because\ everything\ \_should\_\ be\ constant\ folded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04244\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ modern\ compilers.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04245\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04246\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ XOR\ mixing\ hides\ individual\ parts\ of\ the\ secret\ and\ increases\ entropy.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04247\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04248\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ adds\ an\ extra\ layer\ of\ strength\ for\ custom\ secrets.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04249\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04250\ XXH\_FORCE\_INLINE\ XXH\_PUREF\ XXH64\_hash\_t}

\DoxyCodeLine{04316\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04317\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ DISCLAIMER:\ There\ are\ known\ *seed-\/dependent*\ multicollisions\ here\ due\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04318\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ multiplication\ by\ zero,\ affecting\ hashes\ of\ lengths\ 17\ to\ 240.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04319\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04320\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ However,\ they\ are\ very\ unlikely.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04321\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04322\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Keep\ this\ in\ mind\ when\ using\ the\ unseeded\ XXH3\_64bits()\ variant:\ As\ with\ all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04323\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ unseeded\ non-\/cryptographic\ hashes,\ it\ does\ not\ attempt\ to\ defend\ itself}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04324\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ against\ specially\ crafted\ inputs,\ only\ random\ inputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04325\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04326\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Compared\ to\ classic\ UMAC\ where\ a\ 1\ in\ 2\string^31\ chance\ of\ 4\ consecutive\ bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04327\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ cancelling\ out\ the\ secret\ is\ taken\ an\ arbitrary\ number\ of\ times\ (addressed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04328\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ XXH3\_accumulate\_512),\ this\ collision\ is\ very\ unlikely\ with\ random\ inputs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04329\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ and/or\ proper\ seeding:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04330\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04331\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ only\ has\ a\ 1\ in\ 2\string^63\ chance\ of\ 8\ consecutive\ bytes\ cancelling\ out,\ in\ a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04332\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ function\ that\ is\ only\ called\ up\ to\ 16\ times\ per\ hash\ with\ up\ to\ 240\ bytes\ of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04333\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ input.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04334\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04335\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ is\ not\ too\ bad\ for\ a\ non-\/cryptographic\ hash\ function,\ especially\ with}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04336\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ only\ 64\ bit\ outputs.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04337\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04338\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ 128-\/bit\ variant\ (which\ trades\ some\ speed\ for\ strength)\ is\ NOT\ affected}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04339\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ by\ this,\ although\ it\ is\ always\ a\ good\ idea\ to\ use\ a\ proper\ seed\ if\ you\ care}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04340\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ about\ strength.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04341\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04545\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{04546\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04547\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\_accumulate\_512\ is\ the\ tightest\ loop\ for\ long\ inputs,\ and\ it\ is\ the\ most\ optimized.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04548\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04549\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ It\ is\ a\ hardened\ version\ of\ UMAC,\ based\ off\ of\ FARSH's\ implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04550\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04551\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ was\ chosen\ because\ it\ adapts\ quite\ well\ to\ 32-\/bit,\ 64-\/bit,\ and\ SIMD}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04552\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ implementations,\ and\ it\ is\ ridiculously\ fast.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04553\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04554\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ We\ harden\ it\ by\ mixing\ the\ original\ input\ to\ the\ accumulators\ as\ well\ as\ the\ product.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04555\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04556\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ means\ that\ in\ the\ (relatively\ likely)\ case\ of\ a\ multiply\ by\ zero,\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04557\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ original\ input\ is\ preserved.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04558\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04559\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ On\ 128-\/bit\ inputs,\ we\ swap\ 64-\/bit\ pairs\ when\ we\ add\ the\ input\ to\ improve}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04560\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ cross-\/pollination,\ as\ otherwise\ the\ upper\ and\ lower\ halves\ would\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04561\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ essentially\ independent.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04562\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04563\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ doesn't\ matter\ on\ 64-\/bit\ hashes\ since\ they\ all\ get\ merged\ together\ in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04564\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ end,\ so\ we\ skip\ the\ extra\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04565\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04566\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Both\ XXH3\_64bits\ and\ XXH3\_128bits\ use\ this\ subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04567\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04607\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04608\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Multiplication\ isn't\ perfect,\ as\ explained\ by\ Google\ in\ HighwayHash:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04609\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04610\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ Multiplication\ mixes/scrambles\ bytes\ 0-\/7\ of\ the\ 64-\/bit\ result\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04611\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ varying\ degrees.\ In\ descending\ order\ of\ goodness,\ bytes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04612\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ 3\ 4\ 2\ 5\ 1\ 6\ 0\ 7\ have\ quality\ 228\ 224\ 164\ 160\ 100\ 96\ 36\ 32.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04613\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ \ //\ As\ expected,\ the\ upper\ and\ lower\ bytes\ are\ much\ worse.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04614\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04616\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04617\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Since\ our\ algorithm\ uses\ a\ pseudorandom\ secret\ to\ add\ some\ variance\ into\ the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04618\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ mix,\ we\ don't\ need\ to\ (or\ want\ to)\ mix\ as\ often\ or\ as\ much\ as\ HighwayHash\ does.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04619\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04620\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ isn't\ as\ tight\ as\ XXH3\_accumulate,\ but\ still\ written\ in\ SIMD\ to\ avoid}}

\DoxyCodeLine{04622\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04623\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Both\ XXH3\_64bits\ and\ XXH3\_128bits\ use\ this\ subroutine.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{04624\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{05287\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05288\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ XXH3\_scalarRound(),\ GCC\ and\ Clang\ have\ a\ similar\ codegen\ issue,\ where\ they}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05289\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ emit\ an\ excess\ mask\ and\ a\ full\ 64-\/bit\ multiply-\/add\ (MADD\ X-\/form).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05290\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05291\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ While\ this\ might\ not\ seem\ like\ much,\ as\ AArch64\ is\ a\ 64-\/bit\ architecture,\ only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05292\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ big\ Cortex\ designs\ have\ a\ full\ 64-\/bit\ multiplier.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05293\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05294\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ On\ the\ little\ cores,\ the\ smaller\ 32-\/bit\ multiplier\ is\ used,\ and\ full\ 64-\/bit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05295\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ multiplies\ expand\ to\ 2-\/3\ multiplies\ in\ microcode.\ This\ has\ a\ major\ penalty}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05296\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ of\ up\ to\ 4\ latency\ cycles\ and\ 2\ stall\ cycles\ in\ the\ multiply\ pipeline.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05297\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05298\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thankfully,\ AArch64\ still\ provides\ the\ 32-\/bit\ long\ multiply-\/add\ (UMADDL)\ which\ does}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05299\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ not\ have\ this\ penalty\ and\ does\ the\ mask\ automatically.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05300\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}

\DoxyCodeLine{05746\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{05747\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ ===\ \ \ XXH3\ streaming\ \ \ ===\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05748\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#ifndef\ XXH\_NO\_STREAM}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05749\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05750\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Malloc's\ a\ pointer\ that\ is\ always\ aligned\ to\ align.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05751\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05752\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ must\ be\ freed\ with\ \`{}XXH\_alignedFree()`.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05753\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05754\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ malloc\ typically\ guarantees\ 16\ byte\ alignment\ on\ 64-\/bit\ systems\ and\ 8\ byte}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05755\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ alignment\ on\ 32-\/bit.\ This\ isn't\ enough\ for\ the\ 32\ byte\ aligned\ loads\ in\ AVX2}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05756\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ or\ on\ 32-\/bit,\ the\ 16\ byte\ aligned\ loads\ in\ SSE2\ and\ NEON.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05757\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05758\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ underalignment\ previously\ caused\ a\ rather\ obvious\ crash\ which\ went}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05759\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ completely\ unnoticed\ due\ to\ XXH3\_createState()\ not\ actually\ being\ tested.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05760\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Credit\ to\ RedSpah\ for\ noticing\ this\ bug.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05761\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05762\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ alignment\ is\ done\ manually:\ Functions\ like\ posix\_memalign\ or\ \_mm\_malloc}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05763\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ are\ avoided:\ To\ maintain\ portability,\ we\ would\ have\ to\ write\ a\ fallback}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05764\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ like\ this\ anyways,\ and\ besides,\ testing\ for\ the\ existence\ of\ library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05765\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ functions\ without\ relying\ on\ external\ build\ tools\ is\ impossible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05766\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05767\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ The\ method\ is\ simple:\ Overallocate,\ manually\ align,\ and\ store\ the\ offset}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05768\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ to\ the\ original\ behind\ the\ returned\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05769\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05770\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Align\ must\ be\ a\ power\ of\ 2\ and\ 8\ <=\ align\ <=\ 128.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05771\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05772\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ XXH\_MALLOCF\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ XXH\_alignedMalloc(\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ s,\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ align)}
\DoxyCodeLine{05773\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{05774\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT(align\ <=\ 128\ \&\&\ align\ >=\ 8);\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ range\ check\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05775\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT((align\ \&\ (align-\/1))\ ==\ 0);\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ power\ of\ 2\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05776\ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT(s\ !=\ 0\ \&\&\ s\ <\ (s\ +\ align));\ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ empty/overflow\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05777\ \ \ \ \ \{\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Overallocate\ to\ make\ room\ for\ manual\ realignment\ and\ an\ offset\ byte\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05778\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ base\ =\ (xxh\_u8*)XXH\_malloc(s\ +\ align);}
\DoxyCodeLine{05779\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (base\ !=\ NULL)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{05780\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05781\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Get\ the\ offset\ needed\ to\ align\ this\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05782\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05783\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ Even\ if\ the\ returned\ pointer\ is\ aligned,\ there\ will\ always\ be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05784\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ *\ at\ least\ one\ byte\ to\ store\ the\ offset\ to\ the\ original\ pointer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05785\ \textcolor{comment}{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05786\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}\ offset\ =\ align\ -\/\ ((size\_t)base\ \&\ (align\ -\/\ 1));\ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ base\ \%\ align\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05787\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Add\ the\ offset\ for\ the\ now-\/aligned\ pointer\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05788\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ ptr\ =\ base\ +\ offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05789\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{05790\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ XXH\_ASSERT((\textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t})ptr\ \%\ align\ ==\ 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{05791\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{05792\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Store\ the\ offset\ immediately\ before\ the\ returned\ pointer.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05793\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ptr[-\/1]\ =\ (xxh\_u8)offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05794\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ ptr;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05795\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05796\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ NULL;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05797\ \ \ \ \ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05798\ \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05799\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05800\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Frees\ an\ aligned\ pointer\ allocated\ by\ XXH\_alignedMalloc().\ Don't\ pass}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05801\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ normal\ malloc'd\ pointers,\ XXH\_alignedMalloc\ has\ a\ specific\ data\ layout.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05802\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05803\ \textcolor{keyword}{static}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ XXH\_alignedFree(\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}*\ p)}
\DoxyCodeLine{05804\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{05805\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ (p\ !=\ NULL)\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{05806\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ ptr\ =\ (xxh\_u8*)p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05807\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Get\ the\ offset\ byte\ we\ added\ in\ XXH\_malloc.\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05808\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8\ offset\ =\ ptr[-\/1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{05809\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{/*\ Free\ the\ original\ malloc'd\ pointer\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{05810\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ xxh\_u8*\ base\ =\ ptr\ -\/\ offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{05811\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ XXH\_free(base);}

\DoxyCodeLine{06128\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3\ 128\ bits\ (a.k.a\ XXH128)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06129\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ ==========================================}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06130\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH3's\ 128-\/bit\ variant\ has\ better\ mixing\ and\ strength\ than\ the\ 64-\/bit\ variant,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06131\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ even\ without\ counting\ the\ significantly\ larger\ output\ size.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06132\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06133\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ For\ example,\ extra\ steps\ are\ taken\ to\ avoid\ the\ seed-\/dependent\ collisions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06134\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ in\ 17-\/240\ byte\ inputs\ (See\ XXH3\_mix16B\ and\ XXH128\_mix32B).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06135\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06136\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ This\ strength\ naturally\ comes\ at\ the\ cost\ of\ some\ speed,\ especially\ on\ short}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06137\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ lengths.\ Note\ that\ longer\ hashes\ are\ about\ as\ fast\ as\ the\ 64-\/bit\ version}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06138\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ due\ to\ it\ using\ only\ a\ slight\ modification\ of\ the\ 64-\/bit\ loop.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06139\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06140\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ XXH128\ is\ also\ more\ oriented\ towards\ 64-\/bit\ machines.\ It\ is\ still\ extremely}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06141\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ fast\ for\ a\ \_128-\/bit\_\ hash\ on\ 32-\/bit\ (it\ usually\ clears\ XXH64).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{06142\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
